# RECVDATE, STATE, AGE_YRS, VAERS_ID, SEX, SYMPTOM_TEXT, DIED, ER_VISIT, L_THREAT,"

{
    ""query"": {
        ""bool"": {
            ""must"": [
                {
                    ""match"": {
                        ""VAERS_ID"": ""1""
                    }
                },
                {
